CC   This is the CAF1 assembly of the Drosophila sechellia genome. It
CC   has 4.9x coverage. The assembly was improved by using the CAF1
CC   assembly of the Drosophila simulans genome as a reference to
CC   validate both alignments between reads and linkage information. The
CC   gene annotation is based on FlyBase Release 1.3, which contains
CC   some corrections of the original annotation published by the
CC   Drosophila 12 Genomes Consortium.
